### g-request-id-render-bridge-unwired — `<request>` fetches+decodes but the `<#id>` markup render bridge is unwired (data unreachable from markup) — `NEW S213; HIGH; RESOLVED S213 (canonical forms; lift-path → D1/D2)`
A `<request id="x" ...>` (§6.7.7; `url=` OR `api=` mode) emits a fetch into a `var _scrml_request_<id> = { loading, data, error, stale }` object and correctly mutates `.data`/`.loading`/`.error` on resolve — BUT the markup `<#id>` ref does NOT read that object; the two halves are disconnected and every `<#id>` consumption form is broken:
- **`${<#id>.data}` interpolation** → emits `_scrml_input_state_registry.get("<id>").data`, but the request NEVER `.set("<id>", _scrml_request_<id>)` into `_scrml_input_state_registry` → `.get(...)` is `undefined` → runtime throw / silent static shell (compiles GREEN, `node --check` OK — the dangerous "compiled-green ≠ runs" silent class).
- **`<match for=T on=<#id>.data>`** → `E-CODEGEN-INVALID-JS` (the bare `<#id>` token leaks into the match dispatch call). `on=${<#id>.data}` (wrapped) compiles but reads the empty registry.
- **`if=<#id>.X`** → `E-SCOPE-001` (the ref lowers to a bare unresolvable `_scrml_input_<id>_` ident).
- **`const <x> = <#id>.data`** at file scope → broken (parse / module-init level).
- **No reactivity** — even once bridged, `_scrml_request_<id>.data = …` is a plain object mutation (not a reactive cell, no `_scrml_effect` subscription on the markup binding), so post-fetch renders would not update.
**Net:** `<request>` (the whole §6.7.7 surface, not just `<api>`) can fetch + parseVariant-decode but the RESULT cannot be reactively rendered — the canonical "fetch → `<match>`/`<engine>` over loading/data/error" flow is dead. This is the `<api>` arc's real adopter blocker (the A2 W4 fetch+decode codegen IS correct + R26-verified; only the §6.7.7 render-display is gapped — so the §60 Nominal→Implemented flip + the worked example + B-docs are HELD until this lands, user ruling S213). **Empirically confirmed on HEAD `9d30ee93` (S213):** the byob `api=` emit reads `_scrml_input_state_registry.get("user").data` with no matching `.set`; `if=<#user>.loading` → E-SCOPE-001; `<match on=<#user>.data>` → E-CODEGEN-INVALID-JS. **Fix direction (SCOPE-FIRST — possibly architectural):** connect the `<#id>` ref to `_scrml_request_<id>` (register into the input-state registry OR lower the ref to read the request object directly) AND make the request state reactive so the markup binding `_scrml_effect`-subscribes + re-renders on fetch resolve AND fix the `<#id>` ref lowering across the interpolation / `if=` attr / `<match on=>` contexts. Reporter: PA `<api>` dog-food + A2-W5 agent (deferred #1), S213; affects `<request url=>` too. **RESOLVED S213 (merge `fec0a054`, agent a7ebad43 — clean bridge, NOT architectural).** `_scrml_request_<id>` is now `_scrml_deep_reactive`; `<#id>` refs route to it (not the empty `_scrml_input_state_registry`) across interpolation / `if=` / `<match on=>`; bindings `_scrml_effect`-wrapped (reactive re-render on resolve). §36 input-state render-once semantics UNCHANGED. ALSO removed the dead `_scrml_notify` (A2 W4 emitted it 4× but it never existed in the runtime — a latent ReferenceError on every fetch resolve). The **4 canonical forms** (`${<#id>.data}`, `<match on=>`, `if=`, file-scope `const`) work end-to-end in `url=` AND `api=` modes (R26 dual-verified on the merged tree: reads `_scrml_request_<id>` + deep-reactive + effect-wrapped + 0 registry-leak/0 `_scrml_notify` + `node --check`). +20 tests. Landed via 3-way `git merge --no-ff` onto the deep-walk + C1 (S112 stale `ca712295` base; disjoint regions; one stale W5 test-assertion reconciled). **Two lift-path forms DEFERRED → [[g-request-lift-nested-interp-mangle]] (MED) + [[g-request-lift-bare-if-condition]] (LOW).** <!-- @gap id=g-request-id-render-bridge-unwired sev=HIGH status=resolved -->

---

### g-request-lift-nested-interp-mangle — `lift <h1>${<#id>.data}</h1>` nested in a markup-lift block mangles the inner interp — `NEW S213; MED; open`
The S213 `<request>` `<#id>` render-bridge fix ([[g-request-id-render-bridge-unwired]]) wired the 4 canonical forms, but a `<#id>` interp NESTED inside a markup-`lift` block — `${ for (…) { lift <h1>${<#id>.data}</h1> } }` (the §6.7.7 Example-1 shape) — mangles: the emit-lift content-text re-parse splits the inner `${<#id>.data}` into a stray text node (a `crml_input_<id>_` clip + a leftover `"<id>_.data}"`). Two-part root: `emit-lift.js` does NOT thread `requestIds` (so the `<#id>` ref never routes to `_scrml_request_<id>`), AND the lift content-split corrupts the token before routing. **Fix:** thread `requestIds` into `emit-lift.js` + fix the content-split for the `<#id>` `<`/`>` chars (a lift-template / markup-as-value re-parse interaction — high-churn area, a SEPARATE dispatch). Reporter: A2-W5 render-bridge agent (deferred D1), S213. NOTE: §6.7.7 Worked Example 1 is itself STALE (bare `if(){lift}` in `<div>` now needs `${}` wrapping per S204 E-CONTROL-FLOW-IN-MARKUP) — migrate when this lands. **RESOLVED ss15 `8a649853`** — `preprocessWorkerAndStateRefs` (ast-builder.js) made span-aware (skip `<#...>` inside BLOCK_REF child ranges + re-shift); content-split leak killed. §6.7.7 ex.1/2 `${}`-migrated same commit (ss15 item-5; residual `not`/`==not` defects → [[g-spec-677-example-not-and-eqnot-currency]]). R26-verified. <!-- @gap id=g-request-lift-nested-interp-mangle sev=MED status=resolved -->

### g-request-lift-bare-if-condition — bare `${ if (<#id>.loading) { lift } }` reads the §36 registry not `_scrml_request_<id>` — `NEW S213; LOW; open`
A bare `${ if (<#id>.loading) { lift … } }` condition (a `<#id>` ref in a logic-context lift `if`) reads the §36 `_scrml_input_state_registry` rather than the live `_scrml_request_<id>` — the same `emit-lift.js` `requestIds`-threading gap as [[g-request-lift-nested-interp-mangle]]. Compiles, but the condition is never reactive. **Fix:** thread `requestIds` into emit-lift (same dispatch as D1). Reporter: A2-W5 render-bridge agent (deferred D2), S213. <!-- @gap id=g-request-lift-bare-if-condition sev=LOW status=open -->

## §S212 — gaps filed S212 (2026-06-21, flogence dogfood: first browser-render surface)

> Both verified empirically on HEAD `59c15b1e` per the S138 reverse-direction doctrine (reproduce on real source + cross-check the reporter's described reproducer before claiming-open). Both are the compile-clean-but-runtime-broken / silent class, surfaced by flogence's FIRST real browser-render of its cockpit (Surface 2) — prior sessions verified "via the data layer" only, so neither surfaced. The third flogence note (`<each>` in a hidden multi-consumer subtree, MED, lower-confidence/not-minimized) is NOT yet filed — pending minimization.

### g-tailwind-class-scan-skips-markup-block-bodies — the Tailwind class collector never descends into markup block-form `<match>` / `<each>` bodies → utility classes used ONLY inside them get NO CSS rule → silent unstyled render — `NEW S212; HIGH; RESOLVED S212 (a648b34b — collect-class-names.ts match-block/each-block branches)`
The Tailwind JIT class collector (`compiler/src/codegen/collect-class-names.ts`) was written for the OLD `${ for … lift <markup class=…> }` form (see its module header — "control-flow blocks … whose bodies contain `lift <markup>`"). It handles the `${...}`-LOGIC forms (`for-stmt`/`for-expr`/`if-stmt`/`match-stmt`/`match-expr`/`while`/`switch`) + `engine-decl` arms + `lift-expr` — but has NO branch for the MARKUP block-forms `match-block` (`<match for=T on=expr>…arms…</match>`, ast-builder.js:13541) or `each-block` (`<each in=@xs as x>…</each>`, ast-builder.js:14142). Both store their walkable arm/iteration body in **`bodyChildren`** (mirror of block.children; `match-block` also `armBodyChildren`; `each-block` also `templateChildren`/`emptyChild`) — NOT `children`/`body` — so the generic fallback (lines 221-222, `walk(node.children)`/`walk(node.body)`) misses them entirely. Any utility class used ONLY inside a `<match>` arm or `<each>` body gets no generated CSS rule. Green compile, no warning; only visible by rendering in a browser. **Empirically confirmed on HEAD `59c15b1e`** (two minimal repros, `/tmp/tw-triage` + `/tmp/each-triage`): a `<div class="gap-2">` OUTSIDE the block emits `.gap-2`; the arm/body classes (`rounded-full`/`rounded-lg`/`cursor-pointer`/`ml-6` in match arms; `rounded-xl`/`text-sky-500` in an each body) ALL produce NO CSS rule. **BROADER than the reporter's framing** — flogence reported the `<match>`-arm facet (their dashboard wraps the whole body in `<match for=LogPhase>` per the PRIMER §6 errors-as-states pattern → shipped unstyled except classes shared with pre-match markup; 44 rules → 113 after a hoisted-safelist workaround); the `<each>` block-form shares the identical root. This hits the EXACT idiomatic markup-block surface the S210 idiomatic-ification push steers every adopter toward — as the corpus migrates `${for…lift}` → `<each>` / string-flags → `<match>`, in-block styling silently breaks. **Workaround (flogence shipped):** a hidden `<span class="hidden rounded-lg …">` safelist OUTSIDE the block (CSS is global → the rules then apply inside) — marked "DELETE when scrml's extractor descends into arms." **Fix direction:** add a `match-block` branch (walk `bodyChildren` + `armBodyChildren`) and an `each-block` branch (walk `bodyChildren`) to `visitNode`, mirroring the existing `engine-decl` arm branch (the ast-builder comments cite "engine-decl precedent" for these fields). Verify component-slot bodies too (report flagged; CE expands components inline pre-codegen so likely covered — confirm). Dynamic `class="${expr}"` / `class=@cell` stay out-of-scope (documented, W-TAILWIND-001). Reporter: flogence PA (dogfood, Surface 2 cockpit render). **RESOLVED S212 (agent a648b34b, PA S67 file-delta):** added additive `match-block` (walk `bodyChildren` + `armBodyChildren`) + `each-block` (walk `bodyChildren`) branches to `collect-class-names.ts visitNode`, mirroring the `engine-decl` precedent. Nested block-forms (`<match>` in an `<each>` body) + component-slot bodies fall out automatically via uniform `walk` recursion (CE inlines components pre-collector) — both confirmed empirically. PA-independent R26 on the landed tree: match-arm classes (`rounded-full`/`rounded-lg`/`cursor-pointer`/`ml-6`) + each-body classes (`rounded-xl`/`text-sky-500`) all now emit CSS rules; `gap-2`-outside unchanged. +1 value-asserting integration test (`g-tailwind-markup-block-scan.test.js`, 6/6; 4/6 fail against pre-fix source). Full suite 24808/0; within-node unaffected (codegen-output-only). flogence's hoisted-safelist workaround now removable. <!-- @gap id=g-tailwind-class-scan-skips-markup-block-bodies sev=HIGH status=resolved -->

### g-lift-concurrent-transitive-exclusion-tdz — lift-concurrent (§10.5.5) batches a local that TRANSITIVELY depends on an await (through an excluded sync local) into the `Promise.all` → TDZ ReferenceError; a later-reassigned `let` accumulator gets const-destructured → "Assignment to constant variable" — `NEW S212; HIGH; RESOLVED S212 (ad8a0863 — transitive-exclusion closure + body-DG lambda-body free-read fix)`
A CLIENT function that `await`s a server fn (auto-await) then does dependent local `const` computation: the lift-concurrent scheduler (`compiler/src/codegen/scheduling.ts:scheduleStatements`, SPEC §10.5.5) batches sibling initializers into one `await Promise.all([...])` const-destructure. **Same FAMILY as the resolved Bug 56** (the CPS-scheduler TDZ class — `bug-56-cps-scheduler-tdz-and-non-decl.test.js`) **but a DISTINCT, uncovered shape.** Bug 56's fix folds in body-DG edges so a statement that DIRECTLY reads an await-bound local forces a batch boundary — and that part WORKS here (the await-dependent `profiles` is correctly excluded from the batch, declared after it). The gap: the exclusion is NOT propagated TRANSITIVELY — `n = profiles.length` and `scored = profiles.map(…)` depend on `profiles` (a SYNC local that is itself excluded because it depends on the await), and the scheduler still batches `n`/`scored` AHEAD of `profiles`'s declaration → TDZ. **Empirically confirmed on HEAD `59c15b1e`** (`/tmp/lc-triage/repro.scrml`, a `function routeSemantic(query)` calling a SQL-backed `server function loadProfileRows()`): emitted `async function _scrml_routeSemantic_5(query) { const [rows, qtf, n, scored] = await Promise.all([ _scrml_fetch_loadProfileRows_2(), _scrml_tokenize_3(query), profiles.length, profiles.map((pr)=>(…profiles, n…)) ]); const profiles = rows.map(…); return scored; }` — `profiles` is used inside the `Promise.all` BEFORE its `const` declaration. Valid JS (`node --check` clean) → green compile, runtime `ReferenceError: Cannot access 'profiles' before initialization`. **Repro B (sibling facet, flogence-reported, not separately re-minimized):** replacing `n`/`scored` with a `let acc = []` + for-loop accumulator pulls the `[]` initializer into the `Promise.all` and destructures it as `const` → the later `acc = […]` throws "Assignment to constant variable." **Fix direction:** §10.5.5 eligibility needs (1) TRANSITIVE exclusion — a statement is batch-ineligible if it depends, directly OR through any other excluded/non-batched local, on a batched async result (compute the exclusion closure, not just depth-1); and (2) `let`/mutable bindings (or any binding reassigned later in the body) must NEVER be lifted into the `Promise.all` const-destructure. **Workaround (flogence shipped):** isolate the async fetch from the pure compute — move the computation into a pure `fn` (no await to batch around) so the client fn is just `const rows = serverFn(); return scoreProfiles(rows, query)`. Reporter: flogence PA (dogfood, R2 router self-probe threw on every page load). **RESOLVED S212 (agent ad8a0863, PA S67 file-delta) — TWO-LAYER fix (deeper than the single-cause framing above):** (1) `scheduling.ts` — a TRANSITIVE batch-exclusion closure (`depClosure` fixpoint over depSets): a `Promise.all` member may only depend on statements declared BEFORE the batch seed (every transitive dep index < seed `i`), subsuming the prior direct-group-member TDZ check; SPEC-sanctioned (§10.5.5.2 cond 4/5 transitive `awaits` reachability; §19.9.9.2 step-1 absolute must-not-precede). (2) `body-dg-builder.ts` — the RESIDUAL TDZ: `scored`/`n` read `profiles`/`n` INSIDE a `.map(pr=>…)` arrow, but `forEachIdentInExprNode` deliberately STOPS at lambda bodies (a lin-scope boundary — correct for lin, kept untouched); added a body-DG-LOCAL lambda-descending free-read collector (param- + block-local-excluded) so eager-call arrow captures become `reads` facts. (3) Repro B: `collectReassignedNames`/`declIsReassignedLater` gate a reassigned-`let` (lowered as a `tilde-decl`) out of the const-destructure (as candidate AND seed). PA-independent R26 on the landed tree: emit now `const [rows, qtf] = await Promise.all([fetch, tokenize])` then `const profiles = rows.map(…); const n = profiles.length; const scored = …` (profiles declared before all uses; **qtf STILL batches** with the fetch — feature preserved, not over-restricted); `node --check` clean. +1 unit test (`lift-concurrent-transitive-tdz.test.js`, 4/4; latent miscompile → zero fixtures re-baselined). Full suite green incl. self-host 142/0 + e2e-render-map 7/0; within-node 1012/0 unaffected. <!-- @gap id=g-lift-concurrent-transitive-exclusion-tdz sev=HIGH status=resolved -->

### g-nested-each-no-own-subscription — a nested `<each>` (inner each inside an outer `<each>` per-item body) renders one-shot inline and is NEVER registered/subscribed → no reactive subscription to its OWN cell → silent empty render on post-mount cell updates — `NEW S212; HIGH; RESOLVED S212 (a0374ad6 — per-item _scrml_effect; both Tier-1 + Tier-0 nested paths)`
The third flogence dogfood note (filed S212 after PA minimization — originally reported MED / "hidden subtree vs multi-consumer"; root REVISED to NESTED-EACH). An inner `<each in=@inner>` created inside an OUTER `<each>`'s per-item body (`compiler/src/codegen/emit-each.ts`) is emitted as a ONE-SHOT inline IIFE: it reads `_scrml_reactive_get("inner")` ONCE at outer-render time, sets `data-scrml-each-mount="each_<id>"` on its mount, and renders — but it is **NEVER registered in `_scrml_each_renderers[]`** and **NEVER wrapped in `_scrml_effect_static`** (only the OUTER each gets both). So the inner each has NO reactive subscription to its own cell: it renders once with whatever the cell held when the outer each rendered that item, and post-mount updates to the inner cell never re-render it (renders EMPTY if the inner cell was empty at outer-render time — the common load-on-demand case). Doubly orphaned: even the runtime `_scrml_remount_each` (walks `[data-scrml-each-mount]`, re-invokes `_scrml_each_renderers[id]`) finds no fn for the inner id. Green compile, no warning. **Empirically root-pinned via emit inspection on HEAD `59c15b1e`** (no browser needed — the missing registration + subscription is structurally absent in the emitted client.js): `/tmp/each-hidden/nested.scrml` (outer `<each in=@projects>` whose item body has `<each in=@shared>`; `load()` sets `@shared` post-mount) → the inner `each_20` has ONLY the `setAttribute("data-scrml-each-mount","each_20")` line; no `_scrml_each_renderers["each_20"]=`, no `_scrml_effect_static`. **RED-HERRING CORRECTION:** the reporter's "N hidden subtrees share one cell" framing was coincidental — PA confirmed top-level multi-consumer (2 `<each>` on 1 cell, `/tmp/each-hidden/multi-visible.scrml`) AND a top-level each in a `class:hidden` subtree (`/tmp/each-hidden/hidden-single.scrml`) BOTH wire correctly (own renderer + own `_scrml_effect_static` each); neither is the root. The trigger is NESTING — flogence's 3 inner eaches sat inside 3 project cards (an outer each). **Severity HIGH** (silent-wrong-output on a flagship reactivity feature; the nested-`<each>`-over-a-post-mount-updated-cell pattern is common — list-of-cards each with a load-on-demand sub-list / master-detail / expand-to-reveal; the inner each renders correctly ONLY when its cell is populated BEFORE the outer each first renders). Reporter rated MED pre-minimization; upgraded HIGH on the pinned root. **Workaround (flogence shipped):** collapse to ONE top-level `<each>` consumer below the tree instead of N inline ones. **Fix direction:** the inner each must acquire its OWN renderer registration (`_scrml_each_renderers[innerId] = innerRenderFn`) + its OWN reactive subscription (`_scrml_effect_static`) so it re-renders on its cell's updates — OR the each-render machinery must establish a per-mount subscription for nested mounts; mirror how the OUTER (top-level) each is wired in the same emit. Value-asserting regression test (inner cell updates post-mount → inner each re-renders) + ideally a happy-dom render check. Reporter: flogence PA (dogfood, Surface 2 cockpit — expand-a-node → next-layer interaction). **RESOLVED S212 (agent a0374ad6, PA S67 file-delta).** Approach C (NOT the registry/`_scrml_effect_static` fix-direction guessed above — the agent's SCOPE-FIRST analysis rejected it): wrap the inner each's source-read + reconcile in a PER-ITEM `_scrml_effect(() => {…})` inside the outer per-item render closure — which binds BOTH the outer iter var (so enclosing-scope sources `<each in=g.items>` resolve) AND the closure-captured per-item mount (so each instance re-reconciles ITS OWN mount, sidestepping the shared-`each_<id>` problem). `_scrml_effect` un-pauses dep-tracking (S139 Bug 11) so the inner `_scrml_reactive_get` subscribes even though created during the outer paused `_scrml_reconcile_list`. Approach (a) global-registry rejected (per-instance churn → orphan leak); (b) querySelectorAll rejected (can't resolve enclosing-scope sources). **Also fixed the IDENTICAL bug on the parallel Tier-0 `${for…lift}`-nested path** (`emitNestedEachFromMarkup`) — shipping only Tier-1 would have been a partial fix (Rule 2/3). PA-independent R26 on the landed tree: emit-grep shows the inner each wrapped in `_scrml_effect` with the source-read inside (subscribes); the happy-dom regression test (`g-nested-each-no-own-subscription.browser.test.js`) passes **6/6** (4 fail against pre-fix source — inner lists frozen empty after `load()`). Non-reactive enclosing-scope source (`row.cells`, no `@cell`) tracks no dep → effect runs once, byte-equivalent to the old IIFE (no regression). Full suite 24808/0; within-node 1012/0 unaffected. flogence's single-consumer workaround now removable. <!-- @gap id=g-nested-each-no-own-subscription sev=HIGH status=resolved -->

### g-match-arm-drops-reactive-attr-class-effects — reactive `style="…${@cell}…"` templates + `class:foo=(cond)` directives inside a `<match>` arm body emit placeholder markers but NO `_scrml_effect` → silent dead bindings (same arm-body blind spot as the tailwind fix, different pass) — `NEW S212; HIGH; RESOLVED S212 (a0f78a14 — arm-tagged class:/attr-tpl bindings + per-mount _scrml_effect in emitArmWireFunction)`
A reactive `style="…${@cell}…"` attribute template OR a `class:foo=(cond)` directive placed INSIDE a `<match>` arm body compiles green but **never wires its reactive effect**: the arm-render emits the placeholder markers (`data-scrml-attr-tpl-style="…"`, `data-scrml-class-…="…"`) into the arm-render template string but emits **NO `_scrml_effect`** to resolve them — so the binding is dead (the identical construct OUTSIDE the arm wires correctly: `el.setAttribute(...)` + `_scrml_effect`). **Empirically confirmed on HEAD `8dba968e`** (`/tmp/bugB/app.scrml` — `<div style="transform: translateX(${@x}px)">` + `<div class:hidden=(@x>10)>` inside a `<match for=Phase> <Ready>` arm; `bump()` increments `@x`): only **1** `_scrml_effect` in the emit (the OUTSIDE style); the INSIDE arm placeholders `_scrml_attr_tpl_style_3` + `_scrml_class_class_hidden_4` appear ONCE each (in the arm-render template string) with no effect — clicking `bump` moves the OUTSIDE div, the INSIDE div + `class:hidden` never react. **Same arm-body-blind-spot FAMILY as the resolved `g-tailwind-class-scan-skips-markup-block-bodies`** — but a DIFFERENT pass: that one skipped the Tailwind class SCAN of arm bodies; this one skips the reactive-attribute/class/style **EFFECT** codegen. **Root:** the `match-arm-block` render path (`compiler/src/codegen/emit-control-flow.ts` ~1681-1794) renders the arm body to a template string but skips the `_scrml_effect` emission the top-level path (`emit-bindings.ts` / `emit-html.ts`) does — the recurring "arm/iteration render is a separate, incomplete emitter" class (cf. the S212 nested-each fix, the each-peritem gaps). **Severity HIGH** (blast radius: the PRIMER §6 load-phase idiom routes the whole UI through a `<match>` rendered inside the `<Ready>` arm → any reactive `style=`/`class:` in a phase-gated app silently no-ops; green compile, dead binding). Text interpolation (`data-scrml-logic`), `<each>` mounts, and event-handler wiring DO work inside arm bodies — it's specifically the reactive-non-text-attribute-effect pass. **Likely also affects `<each>` block-form bodies** (report flag — verify). **Workaround (flogence shipped):** drive the attribute imperatively from event handlers (which DO wire inside arms) — `document.getElementById(...).style.transform = …`. **Fix direction:** the `match-arm-block` render must collect + emit the `_scrml_effect` for its arm-body reactive-attr/class/style bindings (registered at arm-mount), mirroring the top-level path. Value-asserting test (the INSIDE bindings get an effect + a happy-dom render check: `bump` moves the inside div + toggles `class:hidden`). Reporter: flogence PA (dogfood, Surface 2 cockpit pan/zoom `style` + `class:hidden` drawer, entirely inside `<match for=LogPhase> <Ready>`). **RESOLVED S212 (agent a0f78a14, PA S67 — 3-way apply onto the sibling bare-ref fix `3d311fc9` which touched 3 shared files in disjoint regions, clean auto-merge).** ROOT corrected vs the fix-direction guess above: the `class:`/`attr-tpl` effects are wired ONLY by `emit-bindings.ts` walking `collectMarkupNodes` (`collect.ts:88`), which descends **only `node.children`** — NOT match arm bodies (`armsRaw`/`bodyChildren`) — so the arm-body placeholder was emitted with no effect. Fix (5 files): `binding-registry.ts` +`class-directive`/`attr-template` LogicBinding kinds; `emit-bindings.ts` shared lowering helpers `lowerClassDirectiveCondition`/`lowerAttrTemplateValue` (DRY with top-level); `emit-html.ts` registers arm-tagged directive bindings when `registry.currentArmContext != null`; `emit-event-wiring.ts` SKIPS arm-tagged directives from the global `document.querySelector` init pass; `emit-variant-guard.ts` `emitArmWireFunction` wires them per-mount against `_root` (`classList.toggle`/`setAttribute` inside `_disposers.push(_scrml_effect(...))`). **`<each>` block-form does NOT share the gap** (verified — `emit-each.ts renderTemplateAttrToJs` already wires class:/attr-tpl per-item); generic reactive attrs (`if`/`show`/bool) already wired — only the `class:`/`attr-tpl` directive class (which never reached the registry) was dead. PA-independent R26 on the landed tree: `_scrml_effect` count 1→3, `wire_Ready` now `_root.querySelector` + `setAttribute("style",…)` + `classList.toggle("hidden",…)` in per-mount effects; both flogence fixes COMPOSE (Bug A + Bug B browser tests 16/16). Full suite 24829/0; within-node unaffected. flogence's imperative workaround now removable. <!-- @gap id=g-match-arm-drops-reactive-attr-class-effects sev=HIGH status=resolved -->

### g-bare-ref-event-handler-emits-literal-not-wired — the bare-reference event-handler form `on<event>=handler` (no parens) emits a literal HTML attribute `on<event>="handler"` (a dead handler referencing a nonexistent global) instead of wiring the listener — contradicts normative §5.2.2 — `NEW S212; MED; RESOLVED S212 (abab18f3 — emit-html bare-ref routing branch + bareRefHandler direct-wire)`
The bare-reference event-handler form `onclick=handler` (a bare identifier, no parens) emits a **literal HTML attribute** `onclick="handler"` instead of wiring `handler` as the listener. The bare identifier is the source name; the real fn is module-scoped (`_scrml_handler_N`), so the inline-HTML handler string `onclick="bump"` references a NONEXISTENT global → the handler never fires (and throws `ReferenceError` on the event). **§5.2.2 row 5 is NORMATIVE:** "`onclick=handler` (no parentheses) SHALL wire `handler` directly as the event listener without wrapping." So this is a §5.2.2 conformance BUG (the impl does the opposite of the SHALL), NOT a retire-the-form case — fix-to-wire, per don't-soft-classify. **Empirically confirmed on HEAD `8dba968e`** (`/tmp/bugA/app.scrml`): the bare-ref div emits `onclick="bump"` (literal); the **call form** `onclick=bump()` AND the **expr form** `onclick=${(e)=>fn(e)}` both emit `data-scrml-bind-on…` + a delegated listener (correct). Only the bare-ref form is dead. Silent — green compile, no lint. **Root:** the event-binding collector recognizes the call form (`fn()`) + the `${}` expr form but NOT the bare-ref attribute form `on<event>=<bareIdent>`, so it falls through to literal attribute emission (`emit-html`). NB the `emit-event-wiring.ts:534` bare-ident handling is for the `onclick=${advance}` EXPR form (it appends `()` to invoke a bare ident inside `${}`) — a DIFFERENT path; the bare-ref ATTRIBUTE form never reaches event-wiring. **Fix direction:** recognize `on<event>=<bareIdentifier>` in the event-binding collector + wire `handler` directly as the listener passing the event (no auto-wrap, per §5.2.2 — distinct from the `fn()` call form which auto-wraps `function(event){ fn(); }`). flogence verified mouse/wheel/pointer events (`onmousedown`/`onmousemove`/`onwheel`/`onpointerdown`) DO wire via the call/expr form — the gap is the bare-ref binding form only. Reporter: flogence PA (dogfood, Surface 2 pan handler `onmousedown=startPan` silently did nothing). **RESOLVED S212 (agent abab18f3, PA S67 file-delta).** Root confirmed exactly: `onclick=bump` parses to `{kind:"variable-ref", name:"bump"}` and emit-html.ts's variable-ref branch emitted the literal `onclick="bump"` (the `emit-event-wiring.ts:534` bare-ident path is the separate `${}` expr-form). Fix: NEW else-if branch in emit-html.ts's variable-ref handler — `on*=<bare-non-@-ident>` routes to `addEventBinding({bareRefHandler:true})` (data-scrml-bind-on*) instead of literal emission; emit-event-wiring.ts short-circuits a `bareRefHandler` binding to wire the fnNameMap-resolved `_scrml_<name>_N` DIRECTLY as the listener (NO `function(event){fn();}` wrap — that is the call-form `fn()`; the bare-ref listener receives the DOM event as its arg, per §5.2.2 row 5); +`bareRefHandler` field on the EventBinding interface (binding-registry.ts). PA-independent R26 on the landed tree: bare-ref div emits `data-scrml-bind-onclick` (literal `onclick="bump"` GONE); happy-dom test 8/8 (4 pre-fix-failing — click fires `@n`, non-delegable `onmousedown` fires `@pan`). Call + expr forms no-regress. Full suite 24829/0; within-node unaffected. <!-- @gap id=g-bare-ref-event-handler-emits-literal-not-wired sev=MED status=resolved -->

## §S214 — gaps filed S214 (2026-06-22, scoped-CSS dog-food)

### g-tailwind-lint-false-fires-on-scoped-class — `W-TAILWIND-UNRECOGNIZED-CLASS` fires on a class name the author DEFINED in their own in-scope `#{}` CSS block (the lint only knows Tailwind utilities) → spurious advisory noise on every scoped-CSS-without-Tailwind component — `NEW S214; LOW; OPEN`
The Tailwind utility-class lint (`compiler/src/tailwind-classes.js`, surfaced via `api.js`) warns on any `class="…"` token that is not a recognized Tailwind utility — but it does NOT cross-reference the selectors the author defined in an in-scope `#{}` CSS block (SPEC §9.1 / §25.6 scoped CSS). So the moment you use scoped CSS with custom class names (the canonical without-Tailwind styling path), every such class draws a spurious `W-TAILWIND-UNRECOGNIZED-CLASS` — and the lint message even suggests the `#{}` shim you already wrote. **Empirically confirmed S214** (`/tmp/css-dogfood.scrml`, HEAD `dd5331e2`): a `const Card` with `#{ .card {…} .card-title {…} }` + `<div class="card"><span class="card-title">…` compiles clean and CORRECTLY emits `@scope ([data-scrml="Card"]) to ([data-scrml])` (scoped CSS works end-to-end), yet `card` + `card-title` each draw `W-TAILWIND-UNRECOGNIZED-CLASS`. Advisory only — green compile, correct output; pure NOISE. **Fix direction:** the lint should collect the selector class-names defined in in-scope `#{}` / `<style>` blocks (component-scope + program-scope) and exclude them from the unrecognized-class warning (the same set the `@scope` emitter already resolves). Scope: a pre-pass collecting `#{}` / `<style>` `.class` selectors, threaded into the tailwind-class lint's known-set. **Reporter:** PA scoped-CSS dog-food (S214 — the "is scoped CSS without Tailwind in good shape?" verification). The feature is solid; this is the one ergonomic wart on it. **RESOLVED ss15 `6ad31d8b`** — `findUnrecognizedClasses` (`tailwind-classes.js`) now excludes author-defined in-scope `#{}`/`<style>` `.selectors` (text pre-pass, no AST); +8 tests; R26-verified. <!-- @gap id=g-tailwind-lint-false-fires-on-scoped-class sev=LOW status=resolved -->

### g-typer-render-call-not-in-builtin-allowlist — bare `render()` with NO user `function render` fires a spurious `E-SCOPE-001` in the typer (the call-form `render` builtin is not a typer global, though codegen lowers it fine) — `NEW S214 (sPA ss16 residual); LOW; RESOLVED S215`
Surfaced by sPA ss16 while fixing C3 (render-builtin shadowing). The `render()` client component-render builtin is lowered correctly by codegen, but the typer's scope-checker does NOT register `render` as a builtin global → a bare `render()` call with no user `function render` in scope fires a spurious `E-SCOPE-001`. Orthogonal to C3 (the PongAI/adopter cluster always has a user `function render` in scope, so it never hit this — C3 fixed the shadowing case). **Fix direction:** register `render` in the typer's builtin-allowlist, mirroring the C1/`animationFrame` allowlist class (`LOGIC_SCOPE_GLOBAL_ALLOWLIST`, `compiler/src/type-system.ts`). Pre-existing diagnostic-coverage gap. **Reporter:** sPA ss16 (re-integration residual). **RESOLVED S215 (PA-direct)** — added `"render"` to `LOGIC_SCOPE_GLOBAL_ALLOWLIST` (`compiler/src/type-system.ts`), mirroring the C1/`animationFrame` class; orthogonal to the C3 shadowing fix (codegen still yields to a user `function render`). Reverse-R26 verified: pre-fix `render(42)` → `E-SCOPE-001: Undeclared identifier 'render'`; post-fix clean compile. <!-- @gap id=g-typer-render-call-not-in-builtin-allowlist sev=LOW status=resolved -->

### g-request-lift-bare-if-reads-input-registry — bare `${ if (<#id>.loading) { lift } }` read the §36 input-state registry instead of `_scrml_request_<id>` — `NEW S214 (ss15-4); LOW; RESOLVED ss15 8a649853`

R26-verified. <!-- @gap id=g-request-lift-bare-if-reads-input-registry sev=LOW status=resolved -->

### g-on-mount-bare-call-render-slot — a bare CALL in `on mount { f() }` (default-logic position) mis-collected as a render interpolation → spurious `<span data-scrml-logic>` + `_scrml_render_value(el, f())` (async fn → "[object Promise]") — `flogence dogfood S214; MED→HIGH; RESOLVED ss15 c13bbc48`

### g-control-flow-in-markup-lift-body-evades-diagnostic — `E-CONTROL-FLOW-IN-MARKUP` does NOT fire when the bare control-flow body contains `lift` → silently ships raw `lift …` source text into the DOM — `NEW S214 (ss15 residual); MED; OPEN`
sPA ss15 surfaced (R5 — a diagnostic bug). `E-CONTROL-FLOW-IN-MARKUP` (`ast-builder.js:1518`, gated `block.type==="text"` + `BARE_CONTROL_FLOW_IN_MARKUP_RE`) fires correctly for bare `for(){<li>}` (no lift) but NOT for `<div> if(c){ lift <p>x</> }</>` — the `lift` keyword evades the text-block gate → silent raw-text DOM ship (the same silent-accept class S203's diagnostic was meant to close). **Fix direction:** extend the gate to catch a `lift`-bearing bare control-flow body. **Reporter:** sPA ss15. <!-- @gap id=g-control-flow-in-markup-lift-body-evades-diagnostic sev=MED status=open -->

### g-spec-677-example-not-and-eqnot-currency — SPEC §6.7.7 examples (post-`${}`-wrap) still don't compile clean: `not <#profile>.stale` (E-TYPE-045) + `@appConfig == not` (E-EQ-002) + a pseudo-code body — `NEW S214 (ss15 residual); LOW; RESOLVED S215`
sPA ss15 surfaced (beyond item-5's `${}`-wrap scope). §6.7.7 Example 1 uses `not <#profile>.stale` as boolean negation → `E-TYPE-045` (canonical `!`); Example 2 uses `@appConfig == not` → `E-EQ-002` (canonical `is not`) + a `/* render … */` pseudo-code body. The `not`/`==not` swaps are mechanical (error-message-prescribed); the pseudo-code needs real render content. **Fix:** a §6.7.7 example currency sweep. **Reporter:** sPA ss15. **RESOLVED S215 (PA-direct)** — Example 1 `not <#profile>.stale` → `!<#profile>.stale` (boolean NOT is `!`, not the absence value); Example 2 `@appConfig == not` → `@appConfig is not` (canonical absence-check); the `/* render … */` pseudo-code replaced with real `lift <div class="app"><h1>${@appConfig.title}</h1><p>${@appConfig.tagline}</p></>`. SPEC §6.7.7 Worked Examples. <!-- @gap id=g-spec-677-example-not-and-eqnot-currency sev=LOW status=resolved -->

## §S215 — gaps filed S215 (2026-06-23, giti idiomatic-rewrite findings)

### g-safecall-bang-handler-not-lowered-in-library-mode — `safeCall(...) !{ | ::Thrown(...) :> … }` (§19 host-containment) lowers correctly in program mode but emits the VERBATIM scrml `!{}` handler under `--mode library` → `E-CODEGEN-INVALID-JS` — `NEW S215 (giti F3 / repro-26); MED; OPEN`
giti S15 surfaced (idiomatic-audit rewrite — blocks the canonical try/catch→safeCall replacement in a library module, e.g. `remotes.scrml`'s defensive `JSON.parse`). PA reverse-R26 CONFIRMED on `df6f747b`: `--mode library` emits the raw `safeCall(() => JSON.parse(raw)) !{ | ::Thrown(message, name) :> not }` at byte 238 (the `!{}` call-site error-handler lowering pass does NOT run in library mode) → "Unexpected token"; program mode lowers + compiles clean. The §19 host-containment primitive (the public try/catch replacement) is therefore unusable in library modules. **Fix direction:** wire the `!{}` call-site-handler lowering into the library-mode codegen path (it runs program-mode-only today). **CLUSTER:** library-mode codegen seam — same neighborhood as flogence's library-mode `?{}` db-injection ask (B, §44.7.1 W5a/W5b); consider co-scoping. **Reporter:** giti PA (S15, repro-26). Repro `/tmp/giti-triage/repro-26-f3-safecall-library.scrml`. <!-- @gap id=g-safecall-bang-handler-not-lowered-in-library-mode sev=MED status=open -->

> giti F1 (`E-RI-002` on a server-fn write to an `<engine>` cell) is **WORKING-AS-SPECIFIED** (§12.2 RI — server fns cannot mutate client-side reactive state) → a **server-authority DESIGN question** (server-drivable engine via channel-sync), batched to a dPA session; NOT filed as a bug. giti F2 (SSE bind in `on mount {}`) is **NOT-REPRODUCED** on `df6f747b` — resolved since ca712295 (S214 ss15 on-mount/statement-boundary work).

### g-bindvalue-wiring-dropped-in-match-arm — `bind:value=@cell` on an input INSIDE a `<match>` arm (and SSR-template subtrees) emits the `data-scrml-bind-value` attr but NOT the `querySelector + addEventListener("input")` wiring → typed input never reaches the cell, silent, no error — `NEW S215 (flogence #2); HIGH; OPEN`
flogence cockpit dogfood. The S214 `bind:value` triage closed NOT-REPRODUCED — **correctly for the ISOLATED shape** (top-level input wires 2/2, flogence-confirmed). But the wiring is DROPPED for an input inside a `<match for=Phase>` arm. PA reverse-R26 CONFIRMED on `0d4ba428` (`/tmp/flogence-triage/f2-bindvalue-in-matcharm.scrml`): the `data-scrml-bind-value` attr emits (count 1) but `querySelector('[data-scrml-bind-value=…]')` + `addEventListener("input", …)` is ABSENT (count 0); the same input's `data-scrml-bind-oninput` post-wiring DOES emit (so the post-wiring pass runs — only the bind-VALUE branch is skipped). **Root direction:** the bind:value post-wiring collector does not descend into `<match>`-arm bodies / SSR-template subtrees (same blind-spot CLASS as the S212 tailwind-markup-block-scan + match-arm-reactive-attr-effects — `collect.ts`/`emit-control-flow.ts` arm-body walk). HIGH — `<match>` arms are the canonical Tier-1 UI shape; silent data-loss. **The "adjacent-shape" the S214 isolated repro never tried — live hit of the S215 adversarial-verification doctrine.** **Reporter:** flogence (CORRECTION note, re-verified S10). **RESOLVED S216 (Family-A convergence Half-1, `f4bef40f`)** — extracted root-agnostic `emitBindDirectiveBody` from `emitBindings` + routed arm bind: through `emitArmWireFunction` (`_root`-rooted, `_disposers` teardown); ONE locus (`emitVariantGuardedRender`) fixes BOTH `<match>` arms AND `<engine>` state-child bodies. Half-1's own happy-dom adversarial drive caught a stale-bindId engine-double-render bug (pinned bindId at registration). 24946/0 + 9 browser tests; top-level byte-identical. `<each>` bind: is the separate Half-2. <!-- @gap id=g-bindvalue-wiring-dropped-in-match-arm sev=HIGH status=resolved -->

### g-expr-event-handler-dead-in-each — expression-form event handler `oninput=${(e) => fn(e)}` inside an `<each>` lowers to a built-but-never-invoked arrow (dead); the bare-ref form `oninput=fn(event)` lowers live — `NEW S215 (flogence #4); MED; OPEN`
flogence per-node prompt-box dogfood. PA reverse-R26 CONFIRMED on `0d4ba428` (`/tmp/flogence-triage/f4-each-expr-handler.scrml`): `oninput=${(e) => setQ(e)}` inside `<each in=@rows>` emits `addEventListener("input", function(event) { (e) => _scrml_setQ_1(e); })` — the arrow is a bare expression statement, NEVER CALLED; the bare-ref `oninput=setQ(event)` emits `function(event) { _scrml_setQ_1(event); }` (live). Same FAMILY as the earlier `onclick=${()=>…}`-in-nested-`<each>` dead-handler. **Root direction:** the expr-form event-handler lowering inside `<each>`-arm bodies emits the lambda without invoking it (should wrap-and-call `(arrow)(event)` or unwrap to a direct call). **Reporter:** flogence (CORRECTION #4, tight repro). <!-- @gap id=g-expr-event-handler-dead-in-each sev=MED status=open -->

### g-onmount-async-call-renders-slot — `on mount { asyncCall() }` whose body call is CPS/server-fn-driven (returns a Promise) renders into a slot instead of running as a pure side-effect (`[object Promise]` at runtime; the S214 ss15 on-mount-render fix didn't cover the async case) — `NEW S215 (flogence #5); MED; OPEN`
flogence cockpit boot. PA R26 on `0d4ba428` (`/tmp/flogence-triage/f5-onmount-async-promise.scrml`): `on mount { refresh() }` (refresh = a client fn that CPS-calls a server fn) — the on-mount body leaks into a render slot (PA repro: the literal `on mount { refresh() }` rendered as SSR body text at page top; flogence's browser: `[object Promise]` at runtime). The CPS driver `_scrml_refresh_4` IS emitted; the on-mount handler isn't purely executing it. The S214 ss15 fix covered the sync bare-call on-mount-render-slot but NOT the async/CPS case. Workaround (flogence): wrap in a sync `function boot(){ refresh() }` + `on mount { boot() }`. **Note:** PA repro surfaced an on-mount-block-text-leak (placement-sensitive); flogence's exact `[object Promise]` path is browser-confirmed. **flogence MINIMAL repro DELIVERED (S216 inbox):** the distinguishing shape is `on mount { <fn>() }` as the LAST `${}` statement where `<fn>` is a CLIENT fn whose body assigns reactive cells from SERVER fns (CPS/async) → the on-mount value-slot stringifies the returned Promise → stray `[object Promise]` at page-top. flogence fire-site `src/app.scrml` `on mount { refresh() }` (refresh assigns ~15 cells from `?{}` server fns); Playwright-verified S10 (drop the sync `boot()` wrapper → `hasObjectPromise:true`; restore → false). Trigger = an async-(server-fn-driven)-call AS the on-mount statement vs a sync wrapper returning `undefined`. Repro inbox `handOffs/incoming/read/2026-06-23-from-flogence-onmount-async-repro-for-g-onmount.md`. **This is sub-root D of the S216 seam-investigation** (the emit-html ss15 `DEFAULT_LOGIC_MODE_TAGS` guard not whitelisting the async/CPS on-mount value-slot). **Reporter:** flogence (CORRECTION #5, browser re-verified S10; minimal delivered S216). **RESOLVED S217** (`onmount-cluster-...2026-06-23`, agent aa0c93ee). Root (codegen classification): emit-html classified on-mount POSITIONALLY, but SPEC §6.7.1a/b makes it UNCONDITIONAL — a desugared on-mount/on-dismount is a fire-and-forget effect that NEVER renders in any context. The V0 minimal didn't reproduce because the trigger is the SSR-template PATH (`<program db=>` body → `program>state(db)>logic>bare-expr` → enclosing tag `state` → `inDefaultLogicMode` false → wrong `_scrml_render_value(el, call())` + re-running `_scrml_effect`); flogence's real-app Playwright bisect pinned it. Fix: mark the 4 desugar sites `_onMountEffect`; emit-html skips the render-slot + binding context-independent; closed the re-run-every-update half too. <!-- @gap id=g-onmount-async-call-renders-slot sev=MED status=resolved -->

## §S216 — gaps filed S216 (2026-06-23, surfaced by the Bug-51 /code-review fan-out)

### g-enum-toenum-not-lowered-server-side — `Enum.toEnum(raw)` (§14.4.1/§14.4.3 string→variant DB-coerce idiom) inside a `server function` is NOT lowered to the runtime lookup-table call, AND the `<Enum>_toEnum` / `<Enum>_variants` lookup tables are client-bundle-only → server-side `TypeError: Enum.toEnum is not a function` (compile exit-0, silent) — `NEW S216 (Bug-51 /code-review adjacent); MED; OPEN`
PA empirical-verified at HEAD `a2137214` + the staged Bug-51 fix (`/tmp/bug51-toenum/repro.scrml`): a `server function coerce(raw){ return Load.toEnum(raw) }` emits the VERBATIM `return Load.toEnum(raw);` into `*.server.js` — the §14.4.1 `EnumType.toEnum(x) → (EnumType_toEnum[x] ?? null)` rewrite (`rewrite.ts:1599`, Pass 9 `rewriteEnumToEnum`) does NOT fire on the server-fn path (same client-only pattern the `.variants` → `_variants` rewrite turned out to have) — AND `emitEnumLookupTables` (`const <Enum>_toEnum = {...}` / `const <Enum>_variants = [...]`, `emit-client.ts:1398`/`:2265`) is emitted into `*.client.js` ONLY. So `Load.toEnum(raw)` calls a non-existent method on the frozen `const Load` (the Bug-51 fix DOES emit `const Load = Object.freeze({...})` server-side, but it carries no `toEnum` method) → runtime `TypeError: Load.toEnum is not a function`. `node --check` passes (a member-call is syntactically valid). **SEPARATE from Bug-51** (Bug-51 = the enum DEFINITION absent server-side — RESOLVED; this = the `toEnum` lowering + its lookup table being client-only) and **NOT introduced by the Bug-51 fix** (pre-existing). **giti-RELEVANT:** the §14.4.3 DB-coerce idiom `TaskStatus.toEnum(row.status)` is the canonical "parse a DB string back to an enum variant" pattern; giti's S210-directed enum-`Phase` loaders read DB rows, so if any uses server-side `toEnum()` it TypeErrors. **Fix direction:** (1) run `rewriteEnumToEnum` (Pass 9) on the server-emit path; (2) emit reachability-gated `<Enum>_toEnum`/`<Enum>_variants` lookup tables into the server bundle (extend the Bug-51 enum-emit block to also port `emitEnumLookupTables`, gated on the `_toEnum`/`_variants` identifiers). **Reporter:** PA (S216 Bug-51 `/code-review` finder fan-out — finder-1 surfaced it as the "C1 half-fixed" claim; empirical verify reclassified it from "Bug-51 incomplete" to this distinct pre-existing gap). Repro `/tmp/bug51-toenum/repro.scrml`; flag to giti with the Bug-51 fix-landed notice. <!-- @gap id=g-enum-toenum-not-lowered-server-side sev=MED status=open -->

## §R28 — gauntlet R28 cluster (S143, 2026-05-29)

Overseer caught 2 dev misreports (react+svelte both misreported the transition() path). Detail: `scrml-support/docs/gauntlets/gauntlet-r28-report.md` + `gauntlet-r28/OVERSEER-REPORT.md` + `overseer-verdicts-raw.json` + the 5 dev sources/reports.

**Validation wins (S142 work, all 5 personas, independently confirmed):** errorBoundary §19.6 (nested inner-catches-first, `fallback=`, per-variant `renders` w/ payload, C-hybrid backstop §19.6.8, E-ERROR-005 exhaustiveness) — **zero walls**. Parse gate §2.2.1 default-ON — **zero false positives** across 5 clean compiles + true-positive catches (R28-1 + R28-2). ## §1 HIGH — adopter-visible / silent-wrong-output

> **NEW S140 — Bug-51-class corpus-coverage audit (`docs/audits/bug-51-class-corpus-coverage-audit-2026-05-28.md`).** The audit found 5 silent-miscompiles on shipped features (clean compile + `node --check` pass, but feature wiring absent/broken at runtime), all hidden behind emit-string-only tests with no happy-dom coverage. Bugs **57 / 58 / 59** (HIGH) + **54** (HIGH) filed below; **60** (MED) in §2. Bugs 57/58/59 DISPATCHED S140; 54 + 60 DEFERRED. Each fix's acceptance gate is a happy-dom runtime test (the missing tier that let these ship). PA dual-verified 57/58/59 per pa.md S138 R26 doctrine.
