### G-GIVEN-REBIND-NOT-REJECTED — `given name = expr :>` (SPEC-invalid rebind) not cleanly rejected → E-CODEGEN-INVALID-JS (logic) / silent-accept (markup) — `RESOLVED S189 (E-SYNTAX-045, both contexts)`
<!-- @gap id=g-given-rebind-not-rejected sev=LOW status=resolved -->

**Surfaced S188 dog-food (g-not-neg preserve-surface validation).** SPEC §42.2.3 grammar is `given-guard ::= 'given' identifier-list (':>' | '=>') block` with the prose "No variable is rebound to a new name; each identifier is narrowed **in place**." So the rebind-with-`=` form `given <newName> = <expr> :> body` is INVALID scrml — only `given <existingVar> :>` (narrow-in-place) is valid. But the compiler does NOT cleanly reject the rebind form: **in logic/function context** it emits invalid JS (`E-CODEGEN-INVALID-JS`); **in markup `${}` interpolation context** it SILENTLY compiles (accepts the invalid form). **Isolated (verify-before-claim):** `given n = @name :> n` (named-rebind, expr body, fn) → FAILS (`/tmp/dfn/q1`); `given n = @name :> { @out = n }` (named-rebind, block, fn) → FAILS (`q2`); `given @name :> { return @name }` (unnamed narrow-in-place, fn) → CLEAN (`q3`); `if (@name is some) { return @name }` (the equivalent) → CLEAN (`q4`); the same named-rebind in a MARKUP interpolation (`given s = @selected :> <p>…`) compiles clean (silent-accept). The differentiator is precisely the `<name> =` rebind. **Severity LOW** — canonical `given <var> :>` is unaffected; narrow trigger. **Same "SPEC-invalid form not cleanly rejected" class as [[g-not-negation-unenforced]]** + the misleading-diagnostic family ([[g-markup-const-consumes-cell-decl]], validator-inline-colon). **Fix direction:** reject `given name = expr :>` at parse/type with a clean diagnostic citing §42.2.3 (`given` narrows in place; `= expr` is not a rebind — declare a `const`/`let` first, or use `given <var> :>`), consistently across logic + markup. Repros: `/tmp/dfn/q1.scrml`,`q2.scrml` (fail) vs `q3.scrml`,`q4.scrml` (clean).

**RESOLVED S189 (`g-given-rebind-not-rejected-2026-06-12`, agent `a43899a108317a824`, FINAL_SHA `233dd286`, PA-landed via file-delta).** Fix = a NEW dedicated code **`E-SYNTAX-045`** (the sibling of the property-path reject `E-SYNTAX-044`; NOT an extension of it — property-path is reserved/distinct), fired at BOTH `given-guard` parse sites in `ast-builder.js` (~6680 logic + ~10896 markup) immediately after the existing E-SYNTAX-044 property-path check. Trigger is a bare `=` (`PUNCT`) after a given-bound identifier; `==`/`=>`/`:>` are `OPERATOR` tokens so they never mis-fire (equality / deprecated-separator / canonical-separator). Recovery skips `= <rhs>` to the separator/`{`, keeping the identifier narrowed so multi-var `given a, b :>` still parses. SPEC: §34 catalog row + §17.6 quick-ref + §17.6 SHALL bullet + a §42.2.3 normative "No rebind" paragraph (Rule 4, same commit). **PA-independent R26 (S138):** q1 logic-rebind → E-SYNTAX-045 (the misleading E-CODEGEN-INVALID-JS "compiler defect" path is GONE; a truthful secondary E-SCOPE-001 on the genuinely-undeclared name follows — NOT a spurious cascade); qm markup-rebind → E-SYNTAX-045 (was silent-accept); q3 canonical narrow-in-place → CLEAN; multi-var `given a,b :>` → CLEAN; `given x =>` → only W-GIVEN-ARROW-LEGACY (no double-fire). +192-line regression test (11/11). **Process note:** the agent self-caught + soft-reset an unauthorized `--no-verify` interim SPEC commit, recommitting with the hook; the PA file-delta landing re-runs the pre-commit gate on the PA-authored commit, so the landed state is re-gated regardless. **Surfaced (out of scope, future currency pass):** the E-SYNTAX-044 §34 row carries stale emit-site line numbers `:4440, 7573`.

### G-DIVISION-IN-TERNARY-ARM — a `@cell` consequent/alternative before a ternary `:` truncated the init at `collectExpr` → E-CODEGEN-INVALID-JS in all positions — `RESOLVED S188 (c4cda1ae); MED; collectExpr S25 typed-reactive boundary mis-fire on a ternary value-arm`
<!-- @gap id=g-division-in-ternary-arm sev=MED status=resolved -->

**Surfaced S188 dog-food (channels §38 → derived/expr sweep). RESOLVED S188 (`c4cda1ae` fix + `division-in-ternary-arm.test.js` 15 cases).** A ternary `@e > 0 ? @h / @e : @h` emitted invalid JS (`E-CODEGEN-INVALID-JS`, "compiler defect"). **The original S188 `/`-as-regex / `code-segments.ts` / `rewriteCodeSegments` hypothesis was WRONG (verified-false on the fix worktree):** the tokenizer lexes the arm-position `/` correctly as `PUNCT:"/"` (`isRegexContext()` returns false — the preceding `@h`/operand ends a value), and `parseExprToNode` on the FULL string produces a correct ternary AST. The `/` is a **RED HERRING** — `@e > 0 ? @h : @z` (NO `/` at all) truncated identically, while `@e > 0 ? 1 / 2 : 3` (`/` present, non-`@` arms) was always CLEAN. **Real root (`compiler/src/ast-builder.js`, `collectExpr()` inside `parseLogicBody`):** the S25 typed-reactive boundary break treats a depth-0 `@ident :` as the start of a typed reactive state-decl (`@name: Type` §53). A ternary consequent CAN be a bare `@cell` (`cond ? @cell : alt`), so the depth-0 `@cell :` there is the ternary value-arm separator — NOT a typed-decl start. Mis-firing the break truncated the raw `init` at the consequent (`@e > 0 ? @h /`, dropping `@e : @h`); `safeParseExprToNode` then fell back to an `escape-hatch` over the truncated string, and codegen emitted that raw truncated string (`... 0 ? _scrml_reactive_get("h") /);`). The stale S25 comment claimed "the `:` after `@` cannot appear mid-expression at depth 0 (ternary uses `?`)" — false. **Isolated (verify-before-claim):** trigger is an `@cell` immediately before a ternary `:`; `/` is incidental. `@h / @e` standalone → CLEAN; literal-arm ternary `@e>0 ? 1 : 2` → CLEAN; `*`-in-arm `@a>0 ? @a*2 : @a` → CLEAN; `@cell`-before-`:` → was FAIL. Broad across a local `const x = …` in `${}`, a DERIVED cell `const <ratio> = …`, AND a markup interpolation `${ … }`. **Fix (`c4cda1ae`):** track `ternaryDepth` in `collectExpr` (depth-0+angleDepth-0 `?` opens a ternary, the matching depth-0 `:` closes it; `?.`/`??` tokenize as OPERATOR so optional-chaining/nullish do not perturb the count) and guard the typed-reactive break with `ternaryDepth === 0`, so it fires ONLY for a genuine top-level typed-reactive decl, never inside a ternary arm. The S25 boundary (`@x = 1` then `@y: number = 2` → two decls) still works — `ternaryDepth` resets to 0 once the ternary `:` is consumed. R26-verified: all FAIL→clean (`node --check` clean, correct division emitted), all CLEAN stay clean, `/not found/i` regex verbatim. NOT `code-segments.ts` (untouched). Tests: `compiler/tests/unit/division-in-ternary-arm.test.js`.

---

### G-ATTR-GTE-TAGCLOSE — bare `>=` in an unparenthesized attribute value breaks (leading `>` consumed as tag-close) — `RESOLVED S188 (cluster-A reject+parens; E-ATTR-UNQUOTED-OPERATOR)`
<!-- @gap id=g-attr-gte-tagclose sev=LOW status=resolved -->

**Surfaced S188 dog-food (channels §38 → derived/expr sweep). RESOLVED S188 (cluster-A "reject + parens", `E-ATTR-UNQUOTED-OPERATOR`).** This gap was ONE instance of a broader ~14-operator class: the unquoted-attr-condition scanner silently shredded EVERY bare binary/ternary operator (`>= > < <= == != && || + - * /` + ternary `?:`), not just `>=`. The `>=` form was the LOUD-FAIL sibling (the leading `>` of `>=` closed the tag → misleading E-CTX-001 "no matching tag" cascade); most others SILENT-DROPPED. **User ruling (S188 AskUserQuestion): reject + parens.** A bare operator in an unquoted attribute CONDITION (`if=`/`show=`/`else-if=`) now fires the new `E-ATTR-UNQUOTED-OPERATOR` (§5.2/§17.1/§34) exactly ONCE, naming the operator and steering to the parenthesized (`if=(@n >= 3)`) or quoted (`if="@n >= 3"`) form — both of which handle ALL operators correctly. The atomic unquoted forms (`@var`/`obj.prop`/`fn()`/prefix `!`) stay clean. **Fix:** `block-splitter.js` `>=` early guard (in `scanAttributes` + `peekTopLevelStateDeclSignal`, so the `>` of `>=` no longer closes the opener / mis-reads as a Shape-1 decl) → the run reaches the attribute tokenizer (`tokenizer.ts` `attrConditionOperatorAhead` → `ATTR_OP_REJECT` token) → `ast-builder.js` fires `E-ATTR-UNQUOTED-OPERATOR` + recovers absent (no cascade). R26-verified: `>=` → REJECT once, 0 E-CTX-001. Tests: `compiler/tests/unit/attr-unquoted-operator-reject.test.js` (33 cases). Sibling: [[g-attr-unquoted-compound-silent-drop]] (same fix).


### G-ATTR-UNQUOTED-COMPOUND-SILENT-DROP — `<p if=@x && @y>` (unquoted compound attr condition) SILENTLY drops `&& @y` — `RESOLVED S188 (cluster-A reject+parens; E-ATTR-UNQUOTED-OPERATOR)`
<!-- @gap id=g-attr-unquoted-compound-silent-drop sev=MED status=resolved -->

**Surfaced S188 by the g-not-neg attr-hole follow-up + PA-isolated. RESOLVED S188 (cluster-A "reject + parens", `E-ATTR-UNQUOTED-OPERATOR`).** This gap was the SILENT-DROP face of the same ~14-operator class as the loud-fail sibling [[g-attr-gte-tagclose]]: the unquoted-attr-condition scanner shredded EVERY bare binary/ternary operator. For `&&`/`||`/ternary the RHS operand (an `@`-ref/ident) leaked as a stray attribute (DOM-leak / E-DG-002 "never consumed"); for `>= > < <= == != + - * /` the operator + RHS dropped entirely. **Empirical correction to the original note:** the prior "SPEC §5.5.2 = 4 unquoted forms / compound MUST be parenthesized" framing was a MISREAD — §5.5.2 governs `class:` (E-ATTR-013); `if=` is §17.1 → §5.1/§5.2 (atomic-only unquoted forms). The SPEC was AMBIGUOUS; the user RULED **reject + parens** (S188 AskUserQuestion). **Fix:** the tokenizer (`tokenizer.ts` `attrConditionOperatorAhead`) captures the whole operator run as an `ATTR_OP_REJECT` token; `ast-builder.js` fires `E-ATTR-UNQUOTED-OPERATOR` ONCE, recovering the value as absent — no silent drop, no stray DOM-leaked operand, no E-DG-002. Parens (`if=(@x && @y)`) and quotes (`if="@x && @y"`) stay the canonical operator-condition forms. **Precedence vs prefix-`not`:** for `if=@x && not @y` the binary-operator reject fires first (the more-structural violation — the unquoted compound itself); once parenthesized, the inner `not` then surfaces E-TYPE-045 — never both, never silent. R26-verified: `&&`/`||`/ternary → REJECT once, no E-DG-002, no E-CTX-001. Tests: `compiler/tests/unit/attr-unquoted-operator-reject.test.js`. SPEC: §5.2/§17.1/§34 (new code) + §42.10 reconcile note. Sibling: [[g-attr-gte-tagclose]].

### G-ATTR-IF-FN-CALL-MISROUTE — `if=fn()` (an ATOMIC §5.1 unquoted call condition) wires an event listener instead of rendering conditionally — `RESOLVED S191 (c09b29d2 file-delta; event-binding mis-route FIXED); display-toggle-vs-mount parity filed as [[g-attr-if-fn-display-not-mount]]`
<!-- @gap id=g-attr-if-fn-call-misroute sev=MED status=resolved -->

**Surfaced S188 cluster-A Phase-2 (DEFERRED from the operator-reject core, per brief).** `if=check()` — a bare CALL condition, which SPEC §5.1 admits as a valid ATOMIC unquoted form (`attr=fn()`) and §17.1 should treat as a boolean-call conditional — instead mis-routes to an event binding: codegen emits `data-scrml-bind-if=…` + `addEventListener("if", () => check())` with NO conditional rendering at all (the element always renders; `check()` is never used as a render predicate). **Silent-wrong-behavior** — no diagnostic, the element just unconditionally shows. **Isolated (verify-before-claim):** `if=check()` (this worktree) → `addEventListener("if", _scrml_if_handlers[id])` in client.js (emit-html.ts:1761 `val.kind === "call-ref"` branch unconditionally `addEventBinding({ eventName: name })`, NOT gated on condition-attr names); `if=@n` / `if=(check())` / `if="check()"` → correct conditional render. **Root:** the `call-ref` value branch in `emit-html.ts` (~1761) event-binds for ALL attribute names including `if`/`show`/`else-if`; the conditional-display dispatch (~1679/1708) only handles `variable-ref` and `expr` value kinds. **Why deferred:** routing `if=fn()` as a conditional needs the runtime to RE-EVALUATE `check()` reactively (subscribe to the cells `check` reads internally) — a bare call-ref carries NO direct `@`-refs, so a naive `condExpr: "check()"` would render-once and never update. Correct v1 behavior requires inter-procedural reactive analysis of the function body (which cells it reads) — deeper than the cluster-A scanner fix. **Fix direction:** in `emit-html.ts` gate the `call-ref` branch on `isConditionAttrName(name)` → route as a conditional binding whose reactive subscription is derived from the called function's body-read set (reuse the derived-cell dependency analysis). **Severity MED** — silent-wrong-behavior; clean workaround = parenthesize (`if=(check())`) or quote (`if="check()"`), both of which render conditionally. Sibling: cluster-A [[g-attr-gte-tagclose]] / [[g-attr-unquoted-compound-silent-drop]] (RESOLVED). **S191 survey correction:** the "Why deferred / requires inter-procedural reactive analysis" premise above was a MISDIAGNOSIS — the runtime `_scrml_effect` (which wraps the conditional) does DYNAMIC dependency tracking: the fn is called INSIDE the effect, so the cells it reads auto-subscribe at runtime; ZERO compile-time read-set analysis. The paren form `if=(check())` already works exactly this way, and the conditional codegen already handles empty refs (`emit-event-wiring.ts:947` IS-VARIANT-ATTR comment; effect gates on `subscribeVars !== undefined`, not `.length > 0`). The fix is a small routing change in the `call-ref` branch (gate on if/show, route as a conditional `LogicBinding` mirroring the expr branch). Dispatched S191. **RESOLVED S191 (`c09b29d2`, agent `a4736cab`, PA-R26 dual-verified):** the `call-ref` branch now gates on `name === "if" || name === "show"` and routes a bare call as a conditional `addLogicBinding({ isConditionalDisplay|isVisibilityToggle, condExpr: "fn(args)", refs })` (raw-string condExpr — the fn name is mangled by the whole-buffer `post-fn-name-mangle` pass, so a synthesized CallExpr would emit the unmangled name; the existing `else` event-binding path preserved verbatim). PA-R26: `addEventListener("if")` count 0 (was present); the `if=fn()` site emits a reactive `_scrml_effect` conditional; `node --check` clean; +12 tests; subset 16,885/0. **Remaining (NEW gap, NOT silent-render-wrong):** `if=fn()` lands on the DISPLAY-TOGGLE path (`el.style.display`) whereas `if=(fn())` AND `if=@var` get MOUNT/UNMOUNT — see [[g-attr-if-fn-display-not-mount]]; folds into the chain-head follow.

---

### G-ATTR-IF-FN-CHAIN-HEAD-CALL-MISROUTE — `if=fn()` as an if-CHAIN head (with else-if/else) emits `_scrml_reactive_get("fnName")` instead of calling the fn — chain branch never activates — `RESOLVED S191 (PA-direct; emit-event-wiring.ts:1296 call-ref case)`
<!-- @gap id=g-attr-if-fn-chain-head-call-misroute sev=MED status=resolved -->

**Surfaced S191 dog-food (the g-attr-if-fn-call-misroute waiting-time sweep of the condition-attr region).** The SIBLING of [[g-attr-if-fn-call-misroute]] on the SEPARATE if-CHAIN codegen path. A bare-CALL condition used as an if-CHAIN HEAD — `<div if=isHigh()>…</div> <div else-if=@x>…</div> <div else>…</div>` — lowers the call to `_scrml_reactive_get("isHigh")` (reading the function NAME as a reactive CELL) instead of CALLING `isHigh()`. Since `isHigh` is a `fn` (no `isHigh` cell exists; 0 `_scrml_reactive_set("isHigh")` in emitted JS), the chain-head condition is always `undefined` → the head branch NEVER activates; the chain always falls through to else-if/else. **Silent-wrong-behavior** — no diagnostic. **Isolated (R26, S191):** `if=isHigh()` chain head → `if (_next === null && (_scrml_reactive_get("isHigh"))) _next = "…_b0"` inside the `_update_chain_*` effect (the chain-condition extraction reads the bareword call as a cell key); a STANDALONE `if=isHigh()` is the parent gap (event-bind, `emit-html.ts:1761`) — DIFFERENT manifestation, DIFFERENT code path. The paren form `if=(isHigh())` as a chain head renders correctly (control). **Root:** the if-chain branch-condition extraction (the `_update_chain_*` emitter, separate from the standalone `call-ref` attr branch at ~1761) treats a bare call-ref head as a `variable-ref`-style cell read. **Fix direction:** route a `call-ref` chain-head condition as a CALL (`isHigh()`), mirroring the parent fix's expr-shape routing — the runtime `_scrml_effect` (which already wraps `_update_chain_*`) dynamic-tracks the cells the fn reads, so NO interprocedural analysis is needed (same survey correction as the parent). **Severity MED** — silent-wrong-behavior; clean workaround = paren form `if=(isHigh())`. Sibling: [[g-attr-if-fn-call-misroute]] (standalone — RESOLVED S191 `c09b29d2`). **RESOLVED S191 (PA-direct):** added a `branch.condition?.kind === "call-ref"` case to the chain-condition emitter (`emit-event-wiring.ts` `_update_chain_*`, ~1296) BEFORE the `?.name` variable-ref path — builds `fn(args)` + routes through `emitExprField` (args rewrite, fn name mangled by the post-pass, the wrapping `_scrml_effect` dynamic-tracks). PA-R26: chain head emits `_next === null && (_scrml_isHigh_N())` (mangled CALL), NO `_scrml_reactive_get("isHigh")`; `node --check` clean. Tests in `attr-if-fn-condition-followup.test.js` §2.

---

### G-ATTR-IF-FN-DISPLAY-NOT-MOUNT — `if=fn()` lands on the display-toggle path (`el.style.display`) while `if=(fn())` / `if=@var` mount/unmount — `if=fn()` gives show=-semantics, not if=-semantics — `RESOLVED S191 (PA-direct; emit-html.ts:1394 clean-subtree gate + call-ref binding)`
<!-- @gap id=g-attr-if-fn-display-not-mount sev=MED status=resolved -->

**Surfaced S191 by the PA-independent R26 dual-verify of the [[g-attr-if-fn-call-misroute]] landing (`c09b29d2`).** The S191 fix correctly stopped the event-binding mis-route (the filed symptom — element ALWAYS renders — is gone). But the fix routes a bare-call condition to the `isConditionalDisplay` **display-toggle** path (`emit-event-wiring.ts:965` → `el.style.display = (cond) ? "" : "none"` in an `_scrml_effect`), whereas the equivalent forms `if=(fn())` AND `if=@var` (on a clean subtree) get the **mount/unmount controller** (`_scrml_if_mount`/`_scrml_if_unmount` + template marker). So `if=fn()` behaves like `show=` (§17.2, v-show — element hidden but kept in DOM, subtree scope/effects persist) instead of `if=` (§17.1, conditional render — element unmounted, scope/effects torn down). **Two spec-equivalent atomic forms (§5.1: `@var` / `fn()` / `obj.prop` / `!x`) diverge in render semantics.** **Isolated (R26, S191, side-by-side):** `<p if=isHigh()>` → `el.style.display = (_scrml_isHigh_7()) ? "" : "none"`; `<p if=(isHigh())>` + `<p if=@count>` → `_scrml_if_mount__scrml_if_marker_N()` mount/unmount. The agent's report claimed "`if=@var` also uses display-toggle on a non-clean subtree" — but a clean `<p if=@count>` got MOUNT/UNMOUNT, so the claim doesn't hold for the clean-subtree case. **Root:** the call-ref `addLogicBinding` (emit-html.ts call-ref if/show branch) sets `isConditionalDisplay`/`condExpr`/`refs` but NOT the clean-subtree mount/unmount triggers (`isMountToggle`/`templateId`/`markerId`) that the expr/varref forms acquire — so it falls to the display-toggle emitter. **Fix direction:** make the call-ref condition acquire the same clean-subtree mount/unmount path the expr form gets (so `if=fn()` ≡ `if=(fn())`). Investigate where the expr/varref binding gets `isMountToggle`/`templateId`/`markerId` (the clean-subtree template extraction) and route the call-ref binding through it. **Severity MED** — NOT silent-render-wrong (the element DOES conditionally hide; visible result correct for the common case), but a silent SEMANTIC divergence (unmount vs hide; lifecycle/effect teardown differs) between two equivalent forms; adopter-visible in unmount-sensitive subtrees. Clean workaround = paren form `if=(fn())`. **RESOLVED S191 (PA-direct):** extended the clean-subtree `if=` handler gate (`emit-html.ts` ~1394) to accept `call-ref` + added a call-ref binding branch (mount/unmount `isMountToggle`/`templateId`/`markerId` + condExpr from the call) mirroring the `if=(expr)` form. The two `if=fn()` paths now compose: clean subtree → mount/unmount (this fix); non-clean → display-toggle (the parent fix) — identical to `if=@var` in both cases. PA-R26: clean-subtree `if=isHigh()` now emits `_scrml_if_mount__scrml_if_marker_N` (mount/unmount), no `style.display`. Tests in `attr-if-fn-condition-followup.test.js` §1.

## §8 Where this list comes from

- **Dogfood bug reports** filed when the user/PA hits friction on real adopter-shaped work — see `handOffs/incoming/read/` for archived reports.
- **Spec-vs-impl audit passes** when sweeping a SPEC section (e.g., the S107 §18.0 surface audit that discovered the match block-form gap; the S129 grammar-consolidation Phase 1a/1b/1c audits).
- **Adopter bug reports** (6nz + giti to date; queued in `handOffs/incoming/read/`).
- **PA self-discovery** during implementation work when a planned fix surfaces a deeper gap (e.g., the W-MATCH-RULE-INERT lint attempt surfacing the broader §18.0.1 unparsed state; S130 lifecycle DD surfacing the E-TYPE-001 unimplemented fire).
- **Deep-dive critical findings** (e.g., S130 lifecycle DD's `type-system.ts:1444` per-access transition-state gap).

## §9 Where to discuss / report

- **New gaps in adopter code:** file a GitHub Issue at https://github.com/bryanmaclee/scrmlTS
- **Cross-reference with phase status:** [`master-list.md`](../master-list.md) §0 LIVE DASHBOARD
- **Per-gap implementation arcs:** [`docs/changes/`](./changes/) — each gap with an active impl arc has a SCOPING.md + progress.md there
- **Per-session landings:** [`docs/changelog.md`](./changelog.md)
- **Audit + deep-dive doc inventory:** [`docs/audits/`](./audits/) + `scrml-support/docs/deep-dives/`

### g-sse-route-object-typer-scope — `route.lastEventId` / `route.query` inside a `server function*` SSE body → `E-SCOPE-001 "Undeclared identifier route"` (the synthetic SSE `route` object is not registered in the typer scope) — `NEW S217 (escalation-2 follow-on); MED; OPEN`
Surfaced by the escalation-2 SSE-author-route build (agent a08dc0f5). A `server function*` SSE generator that reads `route.lastEventId` (the resumable-SSE cursor) or `route.query` in its body fires `E-SCOPE-001` — the compiler synthesizes an SSE `route` object at codegen but never registers it in the typer's scope, so the type pass rejects the identifier even though codegen emits it fine. Pre-existing (independent of author `route=`; confirmed against a no-route SSE). Blocks the realistic resumable-SSE FSP shape (`route.lastEventId` cursor) from compiling clean. Fix: allowlist the synthetic SSE `route` object (`.lastEventId`/`.query`) at the typer. Cross-ref escalation-2 `docs/changes/escalation-2-sse-author-route-app-mode-2026-06-23/`. <!-- @gap id=g-sse-route-object-typer-scope sev=MED status=open -->

### g-each-item-hidden-text-stale-flogence — flogence-reported: loop-var `${p.*}` text in an initially-HIDDEN `<each>`-item subtree renders STALE / never reconciles on `@arr` replace — `NOT-REPRODUCED S217; MED; needs flogence LIVE repro`
flogence S11 report (cockpit fleet drawer: `p.deltas`=11 in the cell but `0` in the hidden-then-revealed drawer DOM). The each-cluster agent (a296c101) could NOT reproduce across 5 faithful shapes × 2 set-paths (deep-reactive AND the raw server-load `_scrml_reactive_set(name, rawArray)` flogence emits) × all sequences; even flogence's pre-workaround `app.scrml` shape is byte-identical to a working minimal. The S158 Bug64/R28-1c fix (`af3175e2`, ~3 wks before the report) appears to have already closed this class; `_scrml_reconcile_list` re-fires per-item effects on reconcile. Per R26 discipline: NO fabricated fix — shipped a 6-test GUARD CANARY (`g-each-item-hidden-subtree-text-reconcile.browser.test.js`) locking the current-correct behavior; a future regression of this exact shape goes red. **Owed: flogence LIVE repro** (the trigger may be a flogence-specific runtime condition — SSE/channel-driven `@fleet` set, or a stale dist flogence ran). <!-- @gap id=g-each-item-hidden-text-stale-flogence sev=MED status=not-reproduced -->

### g-each-peritem-markup-value-ternary — `${ @. ? <markup> : "" }` (markup-as-value ternary) in an `<each>` per-item body renders nothing — `NEW S218 (GITI-032 follow-on); MED; OPEN`
The GITI-032 fix routed markup-as-value nested in a ternary through the live `markup-value` node for `<match>`/`<engine>` arm bodies, but the `<each>` per-item path was DEFERRED with a non-regressing skip marker (clean-compile, non-render — same outcome as pre-fix, NOT a loud regression). Needs the `@.` iter-var scope threaded into the markup→DOM build (emit-each `emitCreateElementFromMarkup`/`emitMarkupValueExpr`) so nested refs bind to the iteration item. Dedicated dispatch. <!-- @gap id=g-each-peritem-markup-value-ternary sev=MED status=open -->

### g-nested-interp-in-markup-value-literal — a nested `${@cell}` INSIDE a markup-value consequent (`? <p>${@count}</p> :`) renders LITERAL on both the top-level S201 path AND the arm path — `NEW S218 (GITI-032 pre-existing parity); LOW; OPEN`
Pre-existing (NOT introduced by GITI-032): a `${@cell}` interpolation inside a markup-value ternary branch renders as literal text rather than wiring reactively, on BOTH the top-level S201 markup-value-in-expression path AND the new arm-body path — exact parity. §4.18.4-adjacent. Flag if giti files a follow-up (their status.scrml `<section>` bodies may carry interpolation). <!-- @gap id=g-nested-interp-in-markup-value-literal sev=LOW status=open -->

### g-nested-each-outer-key-reuse-inner-frozen — a nested `<each>` does NOT re-render when its OUTER item node is REUSED on an outer keyed reconcile (same outer key); the inner mount stays frozen at create-time — `NEW S218 (6nz Bug-AI adversarial); MED; OPEN`
Distinct from the S212-RESOLVED `g-nested-each-no-own-subscription` (inner had NO subscription on post-mount cell update): here the inner each HAS its S212 per-item `_scrml_effect`, but when an outer row's node is REUSED on a keyed reconcile (same outer key) and the outer item's iterated field changes (array-replace / field-mutation / push), the inner mount is not re-created/re-bound → stays frozen at its create-time value. Bug-72 / S212 Approach-C residual. Surfaced (verified independent) by the 6nz Bug-AI fix's nested-each adversarial test, which exercised FRESH inner mounts on NEW outer keys (where the bulk-create clear governs). <!-- @gap id=g-nested-each-outer-key-reuse-inner-frozen sev=MED status=open -->

### g-foreign-inline-crossing-shadow — an inline `_{}` `in:{x}` crossing name that shadows a slice-local `const x` emits self-contradictory JS caught as a misleading "compiler defect" E-CODEGEN-INVALID-JS — `NEW S218 (_{} build deferral); LOW; OPEN`
The inline `_{}` codegen emits `(async (x) => { const x = ... })(...)` when an `in:{}` crossing name shadows a slice-local `const` of the same name → invalid JS → validate-emit fires E-CODEGEN-INVALID-JS with the "compiler defect, please report it" message, but it is AUTHOR error (a self-contradictory slice). Recommend a future pre-emit syntactic scan → a clear `W-FOREIGN-CROSSING-SHADOW` / `E-FOREIGN-006`. Surfaced by the dpa-003 build's S215 adversarial pass. <!-- @gap id=g-foreign-inline-crossing-shadow sev=LOW status=open -->

### g-named-machine-arrow-no-statedecl-silent-empty — the §51.3.2 named-machine form (`<engine name=X for=T>`) with a whole-body arrow body and NO separate state-decl still silently renders empty — `NEW S219 (6nz B2 adversarial-review residual); MED; OPEN`
The 6nz B2 fix (`d71a6dcc`, E-ENGINE-RULE-LEGACY-SYNTAX on the whole-body arrow form) is scoped to the §51.0.C state-engine form (`<engine for=T initial=...>`, no `name=`) and EXEMPTS the §51.3.2 named-machine form (`hadNameAttr`) + the `<machine>` keyword + derived engines. But the S219 triage showed `<engine name=PM for=Phase>` + arrow body + NO separate explicit `<phase>: Phase = .A` state-decl ALSO emits no `_scrml_reactive_set` init → governed cell `undefined` at mount → driven `<match on=@var>` renders EMPTY with zero diagnostic — the same silent class B2 fixed for the state-engine form. The named-machine form's canonical pattern supplies the init via a separate state-decl (which is why 6nz p1/p5/p7 work); omitting it is the footgun. Needs either the §51.3.2 named-machine path to emit/require a governed-cell init OR its own missing-init diagnostic. Narrower + lower-priority than the now-fixed §51.0.C case (legacy form + requires omitting the canonical decl); verify §51.3.2 named-machine init semantics before fixing. <!-- @gap id=g-named-machine-arrow-no-statedecl-silent-empty sev=MED status=open -->
